However, Output (a) provides specific information about some London fire staff being on mental health leave after working at Grenfell Tower, which is not mentioned in Output (b). This specific detail makes Output (a) more relevant to the UK context and the fire service in particular.  Considering both the comprehensiveness and relevance of the outputs, it is important to balance these factors when deciding which output is better. While Output (b) is more comprehensive in addressing mental health issues among all emergency service workers, Output (a) is more relevant to the fire service in the UK context. Given the requirement to summarize the key statistics regarding the fire staff's mental health issues mentioned in the article, Output (a) is a more precise execution of the instruction.  Final Decision: Therefore, Output (a) is better.
